Only the sound of the chief's fingertips flipping through the documents disturbed the air settling.

一刀流〝切落〟は敵の一撃に対して全く対称の一撃をもって迎え、これを切り落とし、更に敵の肉体をも断つ技法。　双方が同等の企図をもって打ち合った場合、剣撃の威力と精密さで上回った側が勝利を収める。　今の一合は俺が優越した。　与えた傷は決して浅くない。　これで趨勢が変わった筈！　次の一合で決められるだろう。　　……この男とは、それまでだ。　殺しはしないが動けぬ程に打ち据えて、怪物の相手に向かわねばならない。　そうだ――こんな筋者など。本当は相手取っている場合ではないのだ。　無駄な時間を食わされた……！　返す返すも忌々しい！
Ito-ryu "cut off" is a technique that greets the enemy with a completely symmetrical blow, cuts it off, and cuts off the enemy's body. If both sides meet with the same intention, the side that surpasses the power and precision of the sword attack wins. I was superior in this one. The wounds I gave are never shallow. This should have changed the trend! It will be decided by the next combination. ...... Until then, this man. You have to go to the monster's opponent, not killing it, but striking it so hard that you can't move. That's right-such a person. It's not really the case when you're dealing with someone. I wasted a lot of time ...! It's awful to return!

《――御堂！　敵騎、反転せず！》
《――Mido! Enemy horse, do not flip! 》

《何?》
"what?"

打ち合い、交差した雪車町はそのままに上空へ駆け上がり――上がり続けている。　騎航戦の定石に従うなら、兜角を巡らせて降下へと移り、次の一合に備えて速度を稼がねばならない。　逃げるつもりか。　いや――戦域を離脱するにしても、下方へ向かって速度を得るのが定法。　ならば高度優勢を奪取するための奇手――まさか。　このような方法で上位を取ったところで意味はない。時間が掛かり過ぎる。高度を得、反転、突撃に入ろうとした時には、全てを終えた敵を目前に迎えるだろう。　……あるいは。　逃げの姿勢を見せれば、こちらはすぐに怪物の方へ向かうと踏んだか。　そうしてこちらが下降した隙を狙い、上空から襲う。　――これは、有る。あの男ならばその程度の手管、造作なく用いるだろう。
The snow car town that we met and crossed ran up to the sky as it was-it keeps rising. If you follow the rules of the cavalry battle, you have to go around the helmet angle and move to the descent to gain speed in preparation for the next match. Are you going to run away? No-Even if you leave the theater, it is a standard practice to gain speed downward. Then, a strange move to seize high superiority-no way. There is no point in taking the top position in this way. It takes too much time. When you get altitude, turn around, and try to charge, you'll be greeted by an enemy who's done everything. ...... Or. Did you step on to the monster as soon as you showed an escape attitude? Then, aiming for the chance that this descended, attack from the sky. --There is this. That man would use that kind of skill without any effort.

（乗らぬ）
(Do not ride)

上昇する雪車町の騎影を追う。　間合を詰めるに労はいらない。重力に逆らい続ける敵騎はもはや大幅に速力を失っている。
Follow the rising shadow of the snow car town. No effort is required to close the gap. Enemy horses that continue to oppose gravity are no longer significantly slower.

それでいながら、尚も昇ってゆく。　あまつさえ、兜角を更に引き上げて。　速力という空の戦いにあっては得難い代価を湯尽し、竜騎兵は高度を貪る。　際限なく。止め処なく。飽き足らず。　天頂へ。　届く筈もなき白の円宮を目掛け。　雪車町は何を思うのか。　追尾を受けてなお方針を翻さないのは、ただ諦めの悪さからか。　当方とて速度はみるみる減殺されている。　だが勢力を充分に確保してのち上昇に転じた村正と、太刀打からそのまま上昇に移った竜騎兵との差は厳然。詰まってはいるものの、優劣は明確に有る。　打ち間に捕捉するのは時間の問題。　雪車町が迎撃に転じたとしても、態勢を整える前に斬り伏せられる。　王手を掛けられている事に、彼は気付いている筈だ。　然りながら翔天を止めない。　月の狂気に魅入られ、戦いを忘れたのか――　そんな事さえ思う。
Nevertheless, it still rises. Even Amatsu raises the helmet angle further. The dragoons devour altitude, exhausting the price that is difficult to obtain in the sky battle of speed. Endlessly. Without stopping. Not tired. To the zenith. Aiming at the white circle palace that should never reach. What does Yukishacho think? Is it just because of the badness of giving up that the policy is not changed after being tracked? For me, the speed has been diminished. However, the difference between Muramasa, who secured enough power and then started to rise, and the dragoons, who moved from sword fighting to rising, is severe. Although it is clogged, there are clear advantages and disadvantages. It's only a matter of time before you catch it in between. Even if Snow Car Town turns to interception, it will be cut down before it is ready. He must have noticed that he was checked. However, I can't stop Shoten. Did you forget the fight because you were fascinated by the madness of the moon?

戦慄すべきはその低速域制御力だった。　通常であれば失速していてもおかしくない――いや失速しているべき危険域まで速度を落としながら、彼の見えない手綱は騎体をなお完璧に御している。
What was terrifying was its low-speed control. It's okay to stall normally-no, slowing down to the danger zone where he should be stalling, his invisible reins still control the horse perfectly.

精強さでは人後に落ちない六波羅の正規兵であっても、この域では揚力を手放し、錐揉みして落ちてゆくほかに術を持たないだろう。　百万騎を号す六波羅、その幾人がこの男に倣えるか。　九〇式竜騎兵甲の性能とは到底思われない。　雪車町一蔵の性能に他ならなかった。
Even Rokuhara's regular soldiers, who do not fall behind in terms of strength, will have no choice but to let go of lift and rub them down in this area. Rokuhara, who issues a million horses, how many of them can imitate this man? I don't think it's the performance of the 90-type dragoon armor. It was none other than the performance of Sorimachi Ichizo.

後尾に迫る。　こちらの速力も既に危険域だった。わずかでも気を抜けばその刹那、俺は空から地上へ蹴り落とされるだろう。　間違ってもそんな無様は晒せない。　速度の差はここに至って零に近くなりつつあるも、しかしまだ確在。敵騎はより苛酷な騎航を成し遂げているというに、こちらが先に屈せようか。　あと一歩。　あと一歩で斬れる。
Approaching the tail. This speed was already in the danger zone. If I get rid of it even a little, that moment, I will be kicked from the sky to the ground. Even if you make a mistake The speed difference is getting closer to zero, but it's still there. Enemy horses have achieved more severe voyages, but should we succumb first? One more step. You can cut it in one step.

彼我二騎の描く軌道はもはや垂直上昇に近い。　このような騎航は何秒も保たない。
The trajectory drawn by him is almost vertical. Such a ride does not last for seconds.

騎体の限度だ。　雪車町が――――
It's the limit of the horse body. Snow car town ――――

止まる。　遂に、速度を完全に失い。　倒れる。　横倒しに――　落ちる――
Stop. Finally, I lost speed completely. Fall down. To lie down--fall--

雪車町一蔵は、落ちたのではない。　上昇の極点で、方向翼を切ったのだ。
Sorimachi Ichizo did not fall. At the pole of the ascent, he cut the directional wing.

くるり、と。　魔術めいて鮮やかに、半瞬の間で騎体の上下が入れ替わる。
Quruli. The top and bottom of the horse body are switched in a half moment, vividly with magic.

雪車町の兜角が、重力方向を――　俺を指す。
The helmet angle of Yukishacho points in the direction of gravity-to me.

垂直反転。　上昇速度が無になる刹那の、落下重力の発生を掴み、利用して初めて成し得る所業。
Vertical inversion. A work that can only be achieved by grasping and using the generation of falling gravity in the moment when the ascending speed becomes null.

突如、俺は知った。　何の前触れもなく。何の根拠もなく。　ただ、天啓の閃きで、
Suddenly I knew. Without any warning. Without any grounds. However, with the inspiration of revelation

What is Minato Kageaki's enemy?

It ’s Sorimachi Ichizo.

Time moves. The power of gravity flows.

Now there is no inferiority in Yukishacho. Good posture.

速度比は――逆転する。　何故ならば、純粋な重力が――垂直方向の重力が、雪車町に加勢する。
The speed ratio-reverses. Because pure gravity-vertical gravity adds to the snow-car town.

垂直方向の重力。　俺が今、真っ向から敵にしているもの。
Vertical gravity. What I'm directly enemies with right now.

寸毫の間に始まりそして終わった、完璧な逆転劇。　観客の心境で、既に益体もない知識を引き出す。
A perfect reversal drama that started and ended in the middle of a sword. In the mind of the audience, draw out knowledge that is already unprofitable.

…………あれは。　一刀流の始祖・伊東一刀斎が、師である中条流鐘巻自斎から受け継いだ五つの秘法――
…………That is. Five secret methods inherited from the founder of Ito-ryu, Ito Itosai, from his teacher, Chujo-ryu Kanemaki Jisai.

一刀流の最極意。　妙剣／絶妙剣／真剣／独妙剣……
The ultimate in one-sword style. Mysterious sword / Exquisite sword / Serious / Unique sword ……

そして。　この――――
And. this----

〝金翅鳥王剣〟
"Golden Bird King Sword"

マックス・インメルマン中尉。　外暦一九一四年から一九一八年にわたって戦われた欧州戦争において、比類なき勇名を鳴り響かせた独逸の誇る撃墜王の一人である。
Lieutenant Max Immelmann. He is one of the proud shooting down kings who made an unparalleled heroic name in the European War, which was fought from 1914 to 1918.

その名に〝侯〟の一語が無い事からも明らかな通り、彼は竜騎兵団に属してはいたものの、騎士階級の出身ではなかった。　真打劔冑の継承者ではなかったのである。
As is clear from the lack of the word "Hou" in his name, he belonged to the Dragoons, but was not from the knighthood. He was not the successor to the Shinto Kabuto.

この時代の撃墜王としては異例と云わねばならない。　外暦一九〇〇年代初頭（国紀二五〇〇年代中盤）はまだ数打劔冑が開発されて間もない頃であり、現在に比べれば性能は著しく低いレベルに留まっていた。
It must be said that it is unusual for a shooting down king of this era. In the early 1900s of the foreign calendar (mid-250s of the national era), a few helmets had just been developed, and their performance remained at a significantly lower level than they are today.

彼が愛騎としたフォッカーＥ３とてもそうだ。　張線支持を採用した単翼騎――当時代の技術の粋が凝らされた騎体ではあったが、真打劔冑との性能差を埋めるものでは到底ない。
The Fokker E3 he loved is so. Single-winged horse with support for stretched wire-Although it was a horse body with elaborate technology of the present era, it cannot fill the performance difference with the true hit helmet.

その頃、戦場に華を添えた各国の撃墜王――由緒正しい名門の騎士であり最高の劔冑を継承していた人々――と、一介の騎兵将校インメルマンとの間に、騎体性能の点で巨大な隔絶があったことは確実である。
At that time, the point of horse body performance between the shooting down kings of each country who added glamor to the battlefield-people who were venerable prestigious knights and inherited the best helmet-and one cavalry officer Immelman. It is certain that there was a huge isolation.

しかも、彼の配属された北フランス戦線は敵に正規の騎士が多く、対して味方の騎士は大半が対露戦線に派遣されていたためほとんど皆無という、実に苛酷を極める状況下にあった。
Moreover, the North France front to which he was assigned had many regular knights as enemies, while most of his knights were dispatched to the Russian front, so there were almost no knights, and the situation was extremely harsh.

味方は彼を含めて新弱の竜騎兵ばかり。　敵方は古強の騎士が居並ぶ。　……武功を掲げるどころか、生き残るだけでも至難であったに違いない。
Allies, including him, are all new dragoons. The enemy is lined with old-fashioned knights. It must have been extremely difficult just to survive, rather than to raise martial arts.

その死線にあってインメルマンを撃墜王たらしめたのは、少年期に出会った異国人との体験だった。
At that deadline, it was the experience of a foreigner I met in my childhood that made Immelman the king.

徳川時代の幕引き後、大和はやや閉鎖的であった前時代の反動のように西洋文化を多く取り入れ、何それとなく学んだが、軍事編制においてはプロイセン――ドイツに倣う所が非常に多かった。
After the curtain of the Tokugawa era, Yamato took in a lot of Western culture and learned somehow like the reaction of the previous era, which was a little closed, but in military organization there were many places that imitated Prussia-Germany.

プロイセン軍こそ欧州最精強と見る向きが強かったためである。　幾度となく軍事交流団が派遣され、貪欲に技術知識を求めた。
This is because the Prussian army was strongly regarded as the strongest in Europe. Military exchange teams were dispatched many times and greedily sought technical knowledge.

そうして、ドイツに渡った男の一人に……
Then, to one of the men who went to Germany ...

小野派一刀流一六代宗家、笹木純蔵がいたのだ。
There was Junzo Sasaki, the 16th Soke of the Ono school Ichiroku style.

彼はふとした事から知り合ったインメルマン少年に、一刀流剣術を手解きし、その才の尋常ならざるを知るや、奥義の伝授まで行った。……軽々しいというか、気前が良いというか、いささか変人だったようである。
He learned the Ito-ryu swordsmanship to the Immelman boy he met by accident, and when he learned that his talent was extraordinary, he even taught the mystery. ...... It seems that he was a little weird , light or generous .

だが彼は帰国の後、国粋の文化を売ったとしてこの行為に批判を浴びると、こう応えて一蹴した。　――学ぶのみで教えぬ者は、即ち知恵の盗人である。自分はドイツ軍に学び、返礼として少年に教えたのだ。
However, after returning to Japan, he was criticized for selling the national culture, and he dismissed it in response. --A person who only learns and does not teach is a thief of wisdom. I learned from the German army and taught the boy in return.

かくしてインメルマンは一刀流の秘奥を拝受したのだが、教えた笹木にして彼がその秘技を活用できるだろうとまでは考えていなかったに違いない。
Thus, Immelman received the secret of the one-sword style, but he must not have thought that he could utilize the secret technique with Sasaki who taught him.

一刀流五箇の秘伝は絶えず伝えられてきてこそいたものの、余りの難解さに使い得た者は始祖以来ついになく、技術ではなく単なる知識になり果てていた。　免許皆伝を示す一種の形式に過ぎなかったのである。
Although the secrets of the five Ito-ryu styles have been constantly passed down, no one has been able to use them for too much difficulty since the founder, and they have become mere knowledge rather than technology. It was just a kind of form showing all licenses.

だが、北仏戦線の極限状況にあって――　敵の剛強な騎士に追われたマックス・インメルマンは、差し迫る死に抗う渦中で遂に、秘剣の一つを蘇生させるに至ったのだ。
However, in the extreme situation of the Northern French Front-after being chased by a mighty enemy knight, Max Immelmann finally revived one of his secret swords in the midst of an imminent death.

金翅鳥王剣。　垂直騎航からの反転落下攻撃。　自己より圧倒的に優る敵を討つ、起死回生の剣。
Golden Bird King Sword. Reverse fall attack from vertical cavalry. A sword of rebirth that defeats enemies that are overwhelmingly superior to oneself.

以後、インメルマンは常にこの技と共にあり、幾多の騎士を空から墜として敵味方を瞠目させた。　彼と彼の技は同一視され、その名は欧州を席巻し、悪魔的な恐怖と戦神的な畏怖の的となった。
Since then, Immelman has always been with this technique, dropping many knights from the sky and staring at his enemies and allies. He and his skill were equated, and the name swept Europe and became the target of demonic horror and war-god awe.

一九一六年に戦死するまで、生涯の撃墜数は一七騎。　全てがフランスの名だたる騎士である。
Until he died in 1916, he shot down 17 horses in his lifetime. All are famous knights of France.

現在なおその名は語り継がれ、知らぬ者とていない。　最強、無敵、魔剣、神技――彼の死と共に消え失せた、戦場の幻影を示すものとして、諸国の軍人そして歴史書はその名をいつまでも叫び続ける。
Even now, the name has been handed down, and he is not a stranger. The strongest, invincible, magic sword, divine technique-military personnel and history books of the nations continue to scream their name as an indication of the illusion of the battlefield that disappeared with his death.

〝インメルマンの反転〟と。
With "Reversal of Immelman".

《Mido ………… Are you there?

Muramasa's voice is far away. The field of vision is dull-vermilion. How much damage did you get? Horse body control power to survive the stall. It's more natural than a grudge that no one after him had such a thing. Even though. This man--

The world shakes violently. It also doesn't feel like my own. Probably because there is no pain. Deeply, somewhere in the body should have been torn, but there is no signal from the nerves. Have you been paralyzed yet? Did the brain that should receive the signal break?

これが発生するということは、熱量の欠乏が致命的なレベルに達しつつあるという事。　今、俺の肉体からは血液と共に熱が根こそぎ排出されていっているのだろう。　視野は朧だが、聴覚はまだ鮮明だ。　声が届く。
When this happens, it means that the lack of heat is reaching a fatal level. It seems that heat is being uprooted from my body along with blood. The field of vision is hazy, but the hearing is still clear. The voice reaches.

だから香奈枝は復讐を決行する時、寝込みを襲ったり背後から不意に矢を射込んだりしたことはない。　罪人に抵抗を許し、彼ら自身の正義にかけて戦うのを許し、その上で真っ向から粉砕してきた。
So when Kanae decides to take revenge, she never hits her sleep or shoots an arrow from behind. They have allowed sinners to resist, to fight for their own justice, and then crushed head-on.

断罪と弁明、五分と五分で争う法廷。　そうあってこそ、復讐は正しい。
Condemnation and justification, a court that fights in five and five minutes. Only then is revenge correct.

湊斗景明にも理はある。　彼は彼に為せる範囲で最善を尽くしたという一理が、確とある。
Minato Kageaki also makes sense. There is a certain reason that he did his best to the best of his ability.

短い間ではあったが、香奈枝はその姿を傍らで見てきたのだ。　彼は確かに努力し、力を尽くした。
For a short time, Kanae saw it by her side. He certainly worked hard and did his best.

その苦闘に、　　――――誰も、報いない。
No one rewards the struggle.

彼自身が己の理を主張せず、　香奈枝は相反する理で彼を否定しかしないなら、　　彼の尽力を認める者は何処にもいないのだ。
If he himself does not insist on his own reason and Kanae only denies him on contradictory reasons, then no one acknowledges his efforts.

湊斗景明の苦闘は誰にも受け止められることなく、　無価値なものとして廃棄されてしまう。
Minato Kageaki's struggle is not accepted by anyone and is discarded as worthless.

納得できない。
Unconvinced.

それは怒りにも似た想いだった。　　　　　　　　このまま殺したくはない。
It was a feeling similar to anger. I don't want to kill it as it is.

苛立ちのようでもあった。
It was also frustrating.

そして悔しさ。
And regret.

殺したくない。
I don't want to kill you.

殺したくないならなぜ殺す。

復讐のため？　それにどの程度の価値がある。
For revenge? How much is it worth?

復讐は唯一の正義などではない、　世に数多ある正義のひとつに過ぎないと、とうの昔から知っているのに。
I've known for a long time that revenge isn't the only justice, it's just one of the many justices in the world.

どうしてそれに固執する？
Why stick to it?

どうしてそれに固執した？　……愉しいから。　……そうしたいから。
Why did you stick to it? ...... Because it's fun. ...... I want to do that.

しかし香奈枝は今、　そうしたくないと思ってしまったではないか。
But Kanae hasn't wanted to do that now.

違う。違う。　そうではない。

湊斗景明への復讐はこれまでとは別。　大鳥香奈枝自身の復讐だ。　新田雄飛――　守りたかった子。幸福になって欲しかった子。
Revenge on Minato Kageaki is different than before. It's Kanae Otori's own revenge. Yuhi Nitta-A child I wanted to protect. A child who wanted to be happy.

……守る。
……protect.

そうだ。　俺は守りたいのだ。
That's it. I want to protect.

俺の罪を正しく理解してくれた、　そして正しい罰を約束してくれたあの女性を。
The woman who understood my sins correctly and promised me the right punishment.

何物にも代えて守りたいのだ！
I want to protect it instead of anything!

意識の靄を気力ずくで払い除ける。　上天を睨み、敵影を捕捉する。
You can get rid of the haze of consciousness with your energy. Gaze at the upper sky and capture the shadow of the enemy.
